<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Fixed a binary compatibility issue with <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SemanticsPropertyReceiver.performImeAction</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I658657d6a697e6c5e09cb95500410bd73f237c1b">I65865</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/322269946">b/322269946</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">PopupProperties</code> constructor that takes a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">usePlatformDefaultWidth</code> parameter is no longer experimental. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I8f8d20c49487798766daaa3c64b5be1d3d308c52">I8f8d2</a>)</li>
<li>Added an overload of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ComposeTestRule.waitUntil</code> that takes a string description of the condition to include in the timeout message. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I9413e3f91be4d9754c363d8a8a66ab0e6f72535d">I9413e</a>)</li>
<li>New semantics API <code translate="no" dir="ltr">unset()</code> to remove semantics properties that are added in the same modifier chain. New semantics property <code translate="no" dir="ltr">isOpaque</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I8c583e571956d1501f4df7312a4c60edae0a1bc0">I8c583</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/317966058">b/317966058</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/246056649">b/246056649</a>)</li>
<li>Removed <code translate="no" dir="ltr">originalEventPosition</code> from copy method in public API of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PointerInputChange</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I7beadbea5ea4b5b0125b93f3ceba44006ea58f6b">I7bead</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Fixed an a11y bug allowing non-tabs and non-radiobuttons to be clickable when selected. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I2181c38693bd70e755a7514d655ef9091eef0975">I2181c</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">VelocityTracker</code> will now have the fix for adding points on by default. The fix can still be turned off by setting <code translate="no" dir="ltr">VelocityTrackerAddPointsFix</code> to false if there&#39;s any issues. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ib3877b1f81f19899dd91e20542fa589bf6ed5399">Ib3877</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/269487059">b/269487059</a>)</li>
<li>Fixed backwards binary incompatibility in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TextStyle</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ParagraphStyle</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I179f0ff77b3b85a05d98a28405ad936d2e9413cf">I179f0</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/320819734">b/320819734</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.6.1" data-text="Version 1.6.1" tabindex="-1">Version 1.6.1</h3>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Fixed a backwards compatibility issue with <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SemanticsPropertyReceiver.performImeAction</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SemanticsActions.PerformImeAction</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ie0bb2b112bb585f051db7348e6eaaac859d8660c">Ie0bb2</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/322269946">b/322269946</a>)</li>
<li>Layouts now issue an error while measuring when one returns an abnormally large size. This kind of error normally happens when the measurement uses maximum constraints directly without checking for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Constraints.Infinity</code>. The check will help developers find problems with the layout having the wrong size rather than in a layout that contains it. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/q/I339a906701f382f7e043be65de57af6b9838e695">I339a9</a>)</li>

<h3 id="1.6.0-beta02" data-text="Version 1.6.0-beta02" tabindex="-1">Version 1.6.0-beta02</h3>

<p>November 29, 2023</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.ui:ui-*:1.6.0-beta02</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/1f80a6f0c1cb96288c04124001fa2c9bd29617d6..15c82aaef0f1fd0307d6c00061859e5b6c4384c6/compose/ui">Version 1.6.0-beta02 contains these commits.</a></p>

<h3 id="1.6.0-beta01" data-text="Version 1.6.0-beta01" tabindex="-1">Version 1.6.0-beta01</h3>

<p>November 15, 2023</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.ui:ui-*:1.6.0-beta01</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/465c5c5b7a0d79793bddb26a695f67aba8ea2f7e..1f80a6f0c1cb96288c04124001fa2c9bd29617d6/compose/ui">Version 1.6.0-beta01 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>The <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DragAndDropTarget</code> modifier now takes in the receiving <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DragAndDropTarget</code> explicitly and has a lambda to opt into a drag and drop session. There are now two factory functions for a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DragAndDropModifierNode</code>. One for receiving transfers and one for transferring data (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I69481ca031bfa52b3f8ff910b159e3ee8f7ffaf9">I69481</a>)</li>
<li>Updated <code translate="no" dir="ltr">maximumFlingVelocity</code> to be represented as Float. Updated documentation to be more clear about the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">maximumFlingVelocity</code> unity. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I8adc73327ca3c0d43a9ea31d871ddae1da5e9496">I8adc7</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">onDragAndDropStart</code> in the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DragAndDropModifierNode</code> factory has been renamed to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">acceptDragAndDropTransfer</code>.<code translate="no" dir="ltr">acceptsDragAndDropTransfer</code> has been added to the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">dragAndDropTarget</code> Modifier to accept from a drag and drop session. This lambda returns a viable <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DragAndDropTarget</code> if interested in a drag and drop session. Other lambdas for processing drag events have been replaced by this. a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DragAndDropTarget</code> factory function has been added to receive from drag and drop sessions (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Iebf3a243ad9e4515dfe43b1947ab98ade6804a99">Iebf3a</a>)</li>
<li><p>Removed <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DragAndDropInfo</code> as a type <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DragAndDropModifierNode.drag</code> now takes parameters for the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">transferData</code>, decoration size and drag decoration <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DrawScope</code> lambda</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">DragAndDropTarget</code> has methods for particular drag and drop events instead of being a single abstract method</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">onDragAndDropEvent</code> in the factory function for a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DragAndDropModifierNode</code> has been renamed to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">onDragAndDropStart</code> to better communicate that the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DragAndDropTarget</code> provided is valid for a given drag and drop session only</p>

<p>The <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DragAndDropEventType</code> has been removed (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I645b1531085bceef359daebf7f36aa9119f6017b">I645b1</a>)</p></li>
<li><p>Renamed <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PlatformTextInputModifierNode.runTextInputSession</code> to  <code translate="no" dir="ltr">establishTextInputSession</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I03cd0d84be09a89ed7a763d1b5921cb4975b72a0">I03cd0</a>)</p></li>
<li><p>Improves traversable node api names to make them more understandable. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ia4474e234f77a9e04cfeffd46e7ee6a0f05d006a">Ia4474</a>)</p></li>
<li><p>Replace <code translate="no" dir="ltr">OriginalText</code> by <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TextSubstitution</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ifa5a8d6a2efd776c384642d9148dbf40b23eb6e3">Ifa5a8</a>)</p></li>
<li><p>Renamed <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PlatformTextInputModifierNode.textInputSession</code> to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">runTextInputSession</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ie9c6b37420dc9c024d68bbfc94fdcbbef105a547">Ie9c6b</a>)</p></li>
<li><p>The children of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SubcomposeLayout</code> (and layouts like <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LazyColumn</code> based on it) which are retained to be reused in future are considered deactivated. New <code translate="no" dir="ltr">assertIsDeactivated()</code> test API was introduced to test such nodes. The rests of the test apis will filter out deactivated nodes by default. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I2ef84fb2ed578238bb20c07655c475df6fb8dbd0">I2ef84</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/187188981">b/187188981</a>)</p></li>
<li><p>Removed <code translate="no" dir="ltr">FocusDirection.In</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">FocusDirection.Out</code> use <code translate="no" dir="ltr">FocusDirection.Enter</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">FocusDirection.Exit</code> instead (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I2f660ded2b6e0d018eca7afa0156b9af0ff35316">I2f660</a>)</p></li>
<li><p>Material <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeToReveal</code> APIs (for Cards and Chips) now rely on a slot based API (as recommended by Compose) instead of data class based instances to create those slots. This is a breaking change, please see the demo and sample code for examples on how to use the new API. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ia89431e240b0602bfe08bceb660ff9ef1137d938">Ia8943</a>)</p></li>
<li><p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">FontStyle(int)</code> constructor is deprecated, use <code translate="no" dir="ltr">FontStyle.Normal</code> or <code translate="no" dir="ltr">FontStyle.Italic</code> instead. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I6661037ce4156041740effcc9c194eaa3c55a0c9">I66610</a>)</p></li>
<li><p>Renamed <code translate="no" dir="ltr">FontScalable</code> interface to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">FontScaling</code> (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ie804acee6d71ed8d8fddb6817eea74e5f40da2c6">Ie804a</a>)</p></li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">SoftwareKeyboardController.show()</code> will no longer show the software keyboard if no text editor is focused. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I2165acf1b065cd56e5bfdaab31829e83292efc3c">I2165a</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/301477279">b/301477279</a>)</li>
<li>Hardware key Up events for keys that haven&#39;t received a Down event in the same Compose View will now be ignored. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ib37b434b9275c1e828b980f5124956cc2ef45047">Ib37b4</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/305518328">b/305518328</a>)</li>
<li>Add renderer support for Sweep Gradient in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ArcLine</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I4d5bb5948d2216dca2a29d2449fd97519b2b65bb">I4d5bb</a>)</li>
<li>Implement equals and hashcode for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PageSize.Fixed</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ie3edea3aafd75068cd57c04aafdd7055ead20ad7">Ie3ede</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/300134276">b/300134276</a>)</li>
<li>Fix binary compatibility issue with Window Inset change (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Iee695f0f1b2bf24a820b5a1bccfe550d9c29a5fa">Iee695</a>)</li>
<li>Remove material core layer for Material3 Chip/Button as the microbenchmarks show better performance without it. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I5555573520638dd3c7f0d202e048ae6fffde19e5">I55555</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">TestDispatcher</code>s passed as the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">effectContext</code> to Compose tests will now be used to create the test and frame clocks. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ia71786a741b31b16fa092800732e8c6abcdfcaa5">Ia7178</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.6.0-alpha08" data-text="Version 1.6.0-alpha08" tabindex="-1">Version 1.6.0-alpha08</h3>

<p>October 18, 2023</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.ui:ui-*:1.6.0-alpha08</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/1f7407d4293384a1b91bc142880e3525048b3443..465c5c5b7a0d79793bddb26a695f67aba8ea2f7e/compose/ui">Version 1.6.0-alpha08 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">Modifier.dragAndDrawSource</code> has had the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">onDrawDragShadow</code> lambda renamed to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">drawDragDecoration</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DragAndDropInfo</code> has had the size parameter renamed to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">dragDecorationSize</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Id0e3037697efad03dcf74c2c9393a733e6ab0489">Id0e30</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/303904810">b/303904810</a>)</li>
<li>Introduce <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SemanticsNodeInteraction.isDisplayed()</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SemanticsNodeInteraction.isNotDisplayed()</code> to check if a matched node is visible or not without also asserting on it. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I2c1967befd4ae5dc2fbe324371c3039eecd5d89c">I2c196</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/302100809">b/302100809</a>)</li>
<li>Introduced a special <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Unspecified</code> value for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TextAlign</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TextDirection</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Hyphens</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LineBreak</code> fields of the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ParagraphTextStyle</code> to replace <code translate="no" dir="ltr">null</code>. Because these classes are inline classes, by replacing nullable with the Unspecified, we avoid primitive type boxing. Constructors, getters and other methods in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TextStyle</code> and Paragraph style were updated to accept the mentioned parameters as non-null types. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I4197ea85db556846ecad27ca8f561955e2370951">I4197e</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/299490814">b/299490814</a>)</li>
<li>Add <code translate="no" dir="ltr">GoogleFont</code> overload for reading a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">GoogleFont</code> from XML. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/If8f5911dde550e78bded1a8ea6a72b9e5977bac7">If8f59</a>)</li>
<li>Made <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LoremIpsum</code> <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PreviewParameterProvider</code> an open class. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I41bf5f4e880867aea3603b3c4ea9a37c456e428d">I41bf5</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/266918816">b/266918816</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/300116360">b/300116360</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">FontFamilyResolver</code> now uses <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Dispatchers.Main</code> for cache management coroutines. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ie8dd912e671a4ee49990c76f4d72adad16cc4f53">Ie8dd9</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">AndroidViewBinding</code> now synchronously removes <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Fragment</code> instances inflated by including a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">FragmentContainerView</code> in your layout as part of its <code translate="no" dir="ltr">onRelease</code> by using <code translate="no" dir="ltr">commitNow</code> (instead of the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">commit</code> it was using previously), thus fixing issues with Live Edit&#39;s method with replacing the composition upon changes. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I58fbffefb19ed896ffedc835185718a24a86949e">I58fbf</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.ui:ui-*:1.6.0-alpha06</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/9ce75ea1baa2af10dda8f787f69c40c6654bcac1..91bb8c1f81dcb031bda00fcd8e55f1e890b56f06/compose/ui">Version 1.6.0-alpha06 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Additional optimizations to Material icons. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I3e08d47c8aac295f6ca660cf1d869cc7de01c9e8">I3e08d</a>)</li>
<li>Adds ability to traverse up/down modifier tree to find similar nodes. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I2d2341d3cf02a921983b0b702f33b5bb7cf50675">I2d234</a>)</li>
<li>Added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">onRestoreFailed()</code> callback to the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">focusRestorer()</code> modifier (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ie1d438706b0f302ecba1c969f660359390d01450">Ie1d43</a>)</li>
<li>Added androidx annotations to various graphics APIs to specify <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ColorInt</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">FloatRange</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">IntRange</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Size</code> and more. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Id65c82355bc1859fb2b3683e69606a38779654a5">Id65c8</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/290950582">b/290950582</a>)</li>
<li>Add <code translate="no" dir="ltr">showSystemUi=true</code> to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PreviewScreenSizes</code> definition (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ib61d344d83febde5be9fd2730cc79f2207ece084">Ib61d3</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Behavior Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Compose now uses non-linear font scaling for better readability and accessibility. When font scale &gt; 100% in system settings, small text will increase in size normally, but already-large text will only increase a little bit. Also, line heights defined in SP will automatically adjust to stay proportional to the 100% scale intended height. See the <a href="https://goo.gle/font-scaling-best-practices">Font Scaling Best Practices</a> for more info. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I115181d1e91dff483c68aeb781e7cae4609e73d4">I11518</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.6.0-alpha02" data-text="Version 1.6.0-alpha02" tabindex="-1">Version 1.6.0-alpha02</h3>

<p>July 26, 2023</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.ui:ui-*:1.6.0-alpha02</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/3b5b931546a48163444a9eddc533489fcddd7494..4aed940027a19667e67d155563fc5fa8b7279313/compose/ui">Version 1.6.0-alpha02 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Added a service locator interface that can be implemented by implementors of Composition that allows an implementation of Composition that delegates to another composition delegate service lookups to the original Composition. This should not be called directy and is used to enable creating experimental APIs in the runtime that can be found from wrapped versions of the composer such as the UI module does. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I296b9deae0c30b70d5e37f7b5fa992d2583ef4f4">I296b9</a>)</li>
<li>Completely redesigned <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PlatformTextInput*</code> API. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I6c93a1111561b5cb55c6a34e2fc3738be3c8941d">I6c93a</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/274661182">b/274661182</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/267235947">b/267235947</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/277380808">b/277380808</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">SoftwareKeyboardController</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LocalSoftwareKeyboardController</code> are no longer experimental. <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LocalSoftwareKeyboardController</code> is also now a proper <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CompositionLocal</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I4c3647f331eacc78f15bd5aa6b19a31ff748b23d">I4c364</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">LookaheadLayout</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LookaheadLayoutScope</code> have been deprecated for a few releases and are now removed. The replacement APIs are <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LookaheadScope</code> that can work with any Layout. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I12ac3827e34339ada08c29713558950abc8db5b8">I12ac3</a>)</li>
<li>Added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SemanticsNodeInteraction.requestFocus</code> as a more convenient and discoverable way to request focus in tests. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ie87224a465a60cd462ee0eaf7c2d3797f1d63347">Ie8722</a>)</li>
<li>Add experimental APIs for registering global assertions, for use by testing frameworks in the future. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I12d77ee7f84cf2d6395077d6abef1eb4b634f3df">I12d77</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">AndroidView</code>&#39;s <code translate="no" dir="ltr">update</code> callback&#39;s first invocation will now be defered until the view is attached, instead of running when the composition that introduces the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">AndroidView</code> is applied. This fixes a bug where the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">update</code> callback wouldn&#39;t be invalidated if a state it read was changed immediately by an effect. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ie94381c17c417b4161d1531c9731a3b077ad46fb">Ie9438</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/291094055">b/291094055</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.6.0-alpha01" data-text="Version 1.6.0-alpha01" tabindex="-1">Version 1.6.0-alpha01</h3>

<p>June 21, 2023</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.ui:ui-*:1.6.0-alpha01</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/9eb2d144f9209cb9c4205ad1f981eb7ddf29b96e..3b5b931546a48163444a9eddc533489fcddd7494/compose/ui">Version 1.6.0-alpha01 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>New Features</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Support lookahead in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LazyList</code>. This allows <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LazyList</code> in the lookahead pass to bypass any animation (e.g. item placement animation, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">AnimatedVisibility</code>, etc) and to calculate the lookahead size and position for all children. After the lookahead pass, children of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LazyList</code> could animate independently to the reality as seen in the lookahead pass.</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Behavior Change: includeFontPadding is now false by default in Compose</strong></p>

<p><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/kotlin/androidx/compose/ui/text/PlatformTextStyle#PlatformTextStyle(kotlin.Boolean)"><code translate="no" dir="ltr">includeFontPadding</code></a> is now false by default (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/21d806ccda067df1e0e90cb7a4ff489d7e11a71d">21d806</a>) in Compose. </p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">includeFontPadding</code> is a legacy attribute that controls whether or not to include extra padding on top of the first line and last line of the text to accommodate any characters that may extend above or below the text baselines.</p>

<p>Updating this Compose version will modify how all texts render in your UI by removing the extra padding on top of the first line and last line of every text you display.</p>

<p>Depending on your UI requirements and the font metrics you’re using, the changes should be minimal. However you might encounter blockers such as:
- Broken screenshot tests. Fix the UI if required, and regenerate the golden images.
- Text is slightly misaligned. Remove any custom negative paddings or add padding if required.</p>

<p>You can opt-in to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">includeFontPadding</code> by using <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PlatformTextStyle</code> for each text:</p>
<div></div><devsite-code><pre class="devsite-click-to-copy" translate="no" dir="ltr" is-upgraded syntax="scdoc"><code translate="no" dir="ltr">Text(
 text = myText,
 style = TextStyle(
   lineHeight = 2.5.em,
   platformStyle = PlatformTextStyle(
     includeFontPadding = true/false
   )
   /* … */
  )
)
</code></pre></devsite-code>
<p>You can opt-in to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">includeFontPadding</code> for all your texts by configuring your Material styles. Note that parameter names will vary between M2 and M3.</p>
<div></div><devsite-code><pre class="devsite-click-to-copy" translate="no" dir="ltr" is-upgraded syntax="scdoc"><code translate="no" dir="ltr">val Typography = Typography(
   body1 = TextStyle(
       fontFamily =    /* … <span class="devsite-syntax-gs">*/,</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-gs">       fontSize =    /*</span> … <span class="devsite-syntax-gs">*/,</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-gs">       platformStyle = PlatformTextStyle(</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-gs">           includeFontPadding = false</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-gs">       )</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-gs">   /*</span> … <span class="devsite-syntax-gs">*/</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-gs">   )</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-gs">)</span>

<span class="devsite-syntax-gs">MaterialTheme(</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-gs">   typography = Typography,</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-gs">   /*</span> … */
)
</code></pre></devsite-code>
<p>You can find more about Compose <code translate="no" dir="ltr">includeFontPadding</code> in <a href="https://developer.android.com/jetpack/compose/text/style-paragraph#adjust-line-height">developer documentation</a> and <a href="https://medium.com/androiddevelopers/fixing-font-padding-in-compose-text-768cd232425b">this blog post</a>. </p>

<p>If you experience issues/bugs connected with this change, file a bug using the <a href="https://b.corp.google.com/issues/new?component=779818&amp;template=1371638">issue tracker</a>.</p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Support <code translate="no" dir="ltr">InputConnection#requestCursorUpdates</code> (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I0c69bf50846ad6a639fe3f3f5f77f89747035b26">I0c69b</a>)</li>
<li>Added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">FocusRequester.saveFocusedChild</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">FocusRequester.restoreFocusedChild</code> (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ic557eaacc4b5c5fe9f908c5afcc86fc5e84f2bac">Ic557e</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/272302679">b/272302679</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/275157318">b/275157318</a>)</li>
<li>Add <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ResourceResolutionException</code> type to wrap throwables thrown when attempting to load bitmap assets with a description of the asset path that failed to load. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I19f445605ae8b171532b73b7ae4697cec0453767">I19f44</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/230166331">b/230166331</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/278424788">b/278424788</a>)</li>
<li>Optimized accessibility for performance and memory allocations. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Iede48198c2709b0736a39287ebc8f082d3869ae2">Iede48</a>)</li>
<li>Added semantics properties and actions to support text translation. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I4a6bc0e167389b8604135d05fbcae7b3cebab0d1">I4a6bc</a>)</li>
<li>New property in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">IntrinsincMeasureScope</code> and its implementations (e.g. <code translate="no" dir="ltr">MeasureScope</code>) to indicate whether the current measure pass is a lookahead pass. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I7a8122bf09752d7afb6ace1a0b397a2632708e95">I7a812</a>)</li>
<li>Updated <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DrawScope</code> api to introduce the ability to retarget rendering into a different canvas with alternative density/layoutdirection and size.</li>
<li>Updated <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DrawContext</code> to support configuration of density and layout direction as well as making the canvas configurable. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ie1f9b83f0486bdaa9a159084625c79d312d7e013">Ie1f9b</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/225408150">b/225408150</a>)</li>
<li>Added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Paragraph#fillBoundingBoxes</code> to calculate character bounding boxes. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/If30eee7df01266200e8b41ee3a6efc141f0c781d">If30ee</a>)</li>
<li>Added a set of common <code translate="no" dir="ltr">MultiPreviews</code> (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ia5a27a26c2282a484a91ec812a01a8d1bc1bff17">Ia5a27</a>)</li>
</ul>

<ul>

(<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I940a5fa24ae24dd98ed854eb4b57737c9de857f5">I940a5</a>)</li>
<li>Renamed <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SemanticsPropertyReceiver.performImeAction</code> to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">onImeAction</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SemanticsActions.PerformImeAction</code> to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">OnImeAction</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I8e841b9789b882fecf991ac2fdcfc4fcb0aaa5b7">I8e841</a>)</li>

<li>Added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">asComposePaint</code> API to replace <code translate="no" dir="ltr">toComposePaint</code> as the returned object wraps the original <code translate="no" dir="ltr">android.graphics.Paint</code> (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I22b4c3b279f05277536465f2d5d701030268420f">I22b4c</a>)</li>
<li>Deprecate <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SemanticsProperties.imeAction</code> and replace with a new parameter to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SemanticsActions.performImeAction</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I4a5871554bc5614b494a0ce8a7f60e0357f629aa">I4a587</a>)</li>
<li>Added support for selection by mouse. Touch based selection will expand by word, and shrink by character. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ic0c6c247aefb9cf567525369468fe19fe77dc986">Ic0c6c</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/180639271">b/180639271</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">Paragraph</code> methods that used to throw <code translate="no" dir="ltr">AssertionError</code> for out of bounds offsets now throw <code translate="no" dir="ltr">IllegalArgumentException</code> as <code translate="no" dir="ltr">MultiParagraph</code> does. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I549d3ec936afbd941361690d1f16fadc4998670a">I549d3</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/243338896">b/243338896</a>)</li>
</ul>

<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">LineHeightStyle.Alignment(topRatio)</code> constructor is promoted to  stable API. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I79c3266507757bbb77c238567774ed91761c148d">I79c32</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/261565383">b/261565383</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">TextMeasurer</code> and related APIs are no longer experimental. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I74647908ae270be731ffa12d1599f6c9199fd904">I74647</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/261581753">b/261581753</a>)</li>
<li>Added the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PerformImeAction</code> semantics action to invoke the IME action on text editor nodes. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ic606f69ba8860017a6d11f0f50dc0da063af0512">Ic606f</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/269633506">b/269633506</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">PlatformTextInput</code> APIs are no longer experimental for Android. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I668eba08bb7d2b384ab05f1ef26d490f00ae1bf8">I668eb</a>)</li>
<li>value parameter name for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Enum.valueOf</code> changed (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ia9b89b3c1bd0407c9beac825c49477cdfc9c1f2a">Ia9b89</a>)</li>
<li>more thrown exceptions from enum valueOf (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I818fed80f3a1af1a97b5b0de7882fb2e1b99ae62">I818fe</a>)</li>
<li>Introduced new low-level <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PlatformTextInputAdapter</code> API for building custom text input implementations that talk directly to platform APIs. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I58df46daa7a88f9761dcd711519c6eddf8524b6d">I58df4</a>)</li>
<li>Added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">BlendMode</code> parameter to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DrawScope.drawText</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Paragraph.paint</code>, and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">MultiParagraph.paint</code> methods to support different blending algorithms when drawing text on Canvas. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I57508ab06da481f63b4061ecb8ad72c3a733b0a7">I57508</a>)</li>
<li>Rename <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Font.MaximumAsyncTimeout</code> to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Font.MaximumAsyncTimeoutMillis</code>. Rename only. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I07af50c23dc2c2a640c6297b34b339be79e1a728">I07af5</a>)</li>
<li>Updated DPI values of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">@Preview</code> reference devices (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Id6151d0c71d471824fb86734e5f52f286fa72334">Id6151</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/254528382">b/254528382</a>)</li>
<li>Add <code translate="no" dir="ltr">brush</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">alpha</code> parameters to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">BasicText</code> to allow efficiently animating or setting text brush.</li>
<li>Define box-free lambda types for Float, Double, Long, Int, Short in :ui:ui-unit (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I6f18d24248b890d7c1fd4d0a2fac1c49918b2f2b">I6f18d</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/246961787">b/246961787</a>)</li>

<h3 id="1.5.0-alpha04" data-text="Version 1.5.0-alpha04" tabindex="-1">Version 1.5.0-alpha04</h3>

<p>May 10, 2023</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.ui:ui-*:1.5.0-alpha04</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/01bd392d5702480f8bfe61a8f8bbbea64cf362a0..6f3ac2bd197d5e61ab2708125b57d6ae4003ad68/compose/ui">Version 1.5.0-alpha04 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>New Features</strong></p>

<ul>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">Modifier.Node</code> Delegation Improvements
Added an enhanced ability to delegate to other <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Modifier.Node</code> instances from a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DelegatingNode</code>. This can be done with the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">delegate</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">undelegate</code> APIs. Prior to this change, every API from the delegating node needed to be delegated explicitly to the delegated node. After this change, node interfaces will get delegated implicitly unless the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DelegatingNode</code> is explicitly overriding them. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Icaf30a53c64b3edff6f47aae10add8378081e201">67352bc</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Introduce <code translate="no" dir="ltr">NestedScrollModifierNode</code>, a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">NestedScroll Modifier.Node</code> that can be delegated to. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I69513ed2bbb1b79c24d7e965e609ed5d277a9a87">I69513</a>)</li>
<li>Added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">onReset</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">onRelease</code> parameters to the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">AndroidViewBinding</code> composable, mirroring the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">AndroidView</code> composable and enabling support for View reuse with <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ViewBinding</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I00b1e2a22dde29b6e011d3d8bb1ea51391231856">I00b1e</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/276802519">b/276802519</a>)</li>
<li>Updated Compose Path API to support rewind operations to support usecases of frequent Path manipulation with faster re-use. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I7b797204e20b747fb7510229a220ddf410ca1fd0">I7b797</a>)</li>
<li>Added optimized <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TextStyle.merge(...)</code> with full parameter list. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Iad23419809af1c7405ba9a9d42569521e7647034">Iad234</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/246961787">b/246961787</a>)</li>
<li>Stabilized many Text APIs that include <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Brush</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DrawStyle</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TextMotion</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DrawScope.drawText</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Paragraph.paint(Brush)</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">MultiParagraph.paint(Brush)</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I2f7409cb64ade53b1ebc3385293456b126314b14">I2f740</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/261581564">b/261581564</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/261581931">b/261581931</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/261561245">b/261561245</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">PlatformTextStyle.includeFontPadding</code> is undeprecated. Our original intent was to remove the field, however the feedback shows that developers need this configuration option. Therefore removing deprecation from the field (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I98e96222691d8e5d023cd22b899f0dfbae2a1e1d">I98e96</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/277703184">b/277703184</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Fixed regression where keyboard wasn&#39;t showing for text fields inside dialogs not created by the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Dialog</code> composable. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I825512cde7e41dadfc8b7491bd24190d21b14729">I82551</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/262140644">b/262140644</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.5.0-alpha03" data-text="Version 1.5.0-alpha03" tabindex="-1">Version 1.5.0-alpha03</h3>

<p>April 19, 2023</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.ui:ui-*:1.5.0-alpha03</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/a200cb82769634cecdb118ec4f0bfdf0b086e597..01bd392d5702480f8bfe61a8f8bbbea64cf362a0/compose/ui">Version 1.5.0-alpha03 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>New Features</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>New default behavior for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SubcomposeLayout</code> in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LookaheadScope</code>: <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SubcomposeLayouts</code> that don’t have conditional slots (e.g. <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TabRow</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Scaffold</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">BoxWithConstraints</code>, etc) now work nicely with lookahead animations.</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>New default <code translate="no" dir="ltr">intermediateMeasurePolicy</code> that reuses measure policy from lookahead pass allows <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SubcomposeLayout</code> subtypes without conditional slots such as <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Scaffold</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TabRow</code>, and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">BoxWithConstraints</code> to work with lookahead by default. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Id84c8357e63905ea09b07acee91094489eb04402">Id84c8</a>)</li>
<li>The recomposer created for an Android window will now only block calls to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">withFrameNanos</code> instead of all composition when it receives an <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ON_STOP</code> notification. This means windows associated with stopped activites will continue to recompose for data changes but the animations, or any other caller of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">withFrameNanos</code>, will block. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Id9e7fe262710544a48c2e4fc5fcbf1d27bfaa1ba">Id9e7f</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/240975572">b/240975572</a>)</li>
<li>Changes <code translate="no" dir="ltr">motionEventSpy</code> to stable. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ic5ec4ef446908ae7fca45c5d3c6c816b61a8029f">Ic5ec4</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/261560988">b/261560988</a>)</li>
<li>Added public <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TextRange.constrain</code> method. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I97912f1c1492f877bdeb9e0369e7be6f7f6a1420">I97912</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">PlatformTextStyle.includeFontPadding</code> is no longer deprecated to encourage developers to use this compatibility API to switch and test setting <code translate="no" dir="ltr">includeFontPadding</code> false. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I98e96222691d8e5d023cd22b899f0dfbae2a1e1d">I98e96</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/277703184">b/277703184</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.5.0-alpha02" data-text="Version 1.5.0-alpha02" tabindex="-1">Version 1.5.0-alpha02</h3>

<p>April 5, 2023</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.ui:ui-*:1.5.0-alpha02</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/5e7d256f82fbafb6d059ab7b18fddd87c7531553..a200cb82769634cecdb118ec4f0bfdf0b086e597/compose/ui">Version 1.5.0-alpha02 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>New <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SubcomposeLayout</code> API that takes an additional intermediate measure policy for handling measure/layout logic during lookahead-based animations. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I017d37b9d3c2f890387229bc8cfc6515913c1a3a">I017d3</a>)</li>
<li>PointerInput is now lazy and uses Modifier.Node for better performance (<a href="https://medium.com/androiddevelopers/improvements-and-changes-to-composes-pointer-input-6026904ac972">read about the minor behavior change</a>). (<a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+/15dab9f17ec9b6b79e1a3d8324393a900019af7c">15dab9</a>)</li>
<li>Changes experimental APIs to stable with Key events. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I9c7d8b826cd7f92a06e76136441892346a495b8e">I9c7d8</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/261566839">b/261566839</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/261567368">b/261567368</a>)</li>
<li>Changes experimental APIs to stable in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PointerInputChange</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I1b5430f6bece9ee985a2a45b820dd5e5334832ec">I1b543</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/261560988">b/261560988</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/261565762">b/261565762</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/261565749">b/261565749</a>)</li>
<li>Adds a way to instantiate a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SuspendingPointerInputModifierNode</code> for more complex <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Modifier.Node</code> implementations. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ic493335d030a524eac7297ad620041bbc13e00d8">Ic4933</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">UrlAnnotation</code>s in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">AnnotatedString</code>s can now be opened via accessibility services like <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TalkBack</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/If4d82999d8c62aa3718e1e681eeeaac12a9b0f55">If4d82</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/253292081">b/253292081</a>)</li>
<li>Added an API to intercept hardware keys before they are sent to the soft keyboard (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I4f4c62841c98d26c654ca34505379ac6a3aa3136">I4f4c6</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/186800395">b/186800395</a>)</li>
<li>Added the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">InsertTextAtCursor</code> semantics action for text fields. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I11ed573be29737b234a114863c3c8f81e0fd65b1">I11ed5</a>)</li>
<li>Text-related test actions (e.g. <code translate="no" dir="ltr">performTextInput</code>) will now request focus directly, using the semantics action, instead of clicking on the field. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I6ed05394845155b1a7335e341ed3548a322f04f5">I6ed05</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>

<h3 id="1.5.0-alpha01" data-text="Version 1.5.0-alpha01" tabindex="-1">Version 1.5.0-alpha01</h3>

<p>March 22, 2023</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.ui:ui-*:1.5.0-alpha01</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/5e7d256f82fbafb6d059ab7b18fddd87c7531553/compose/ui">Version 1.5.0-alpha01 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Modifier.intermediateLayout now doesn&#39;t require an explicit LookaheadScope. The measure block in intermediateLayout has IntermediateMeasureScope as receiver, which provides convenient CoroutineScope, LookaheadScope and MeasureScope.(<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ibe2e5e20a833d3824213e86e5c1e155f65647ad7">Ibe2e5</a>)</li>
<li>LookaheadLayout has been replaced by LookaheadScope, which is no longer a Layout. This allows chid content in a LookaheadScope to be directly controlled by parent&#39;s MeasurePolicy. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ibe2e5e20a833d3824213e86e5c1e155f65647ad7">Ibe2e5</a>)</li>
<li>Adds <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Modifier.Node#coroutineScope</code> to allow Modifier.Nodes to launch coroutines. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I76ef9c67fb270c8d6ba4f7ccfd5379fdf7d2db69">I76ef9</a>)</li>
<li>Allow Modifier.Nodes to read CompositionLocals by implementing the CompositionLocalConsumerModifierNode interface. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ib44df147ceaad520c9102c416440d20fadadc403">Ib44df</a>)</li>
<li>Propagation of @Deprecated class to property. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I882d15d1d0d17f2227262e682d05d9dc7d082e8a">I882d1</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.4.0" data-text="Version 1.4.0" tabindex="-1">Version 1.4.0</h3>

<p>March 22, 2023</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.ui:ui-*:1.4.0</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/548c8ac2570ae6cf15798fea1380491f7d93796b..c5b142d6ab0494c996b2378d5008ac1cd6da75f3/compose/ui">Version 1.4.0 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>Important changes since 1.3.0</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Added a new <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PinnableContainer</code> API that allows lazy list items to be pinned, so that they are not disposed when they are scrolled out of bounds. For example, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Modifier.focusable()</code> uses this mechanism to pin the currently focused item. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ib8881191a529c9d9dc5e886570650b1987763207">Ib8881</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/259274257">b/259274257</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/195049010">b/195049010</a>)</li>
<li>The focus system is rewritten using the new experimental <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Modifier.Node</code> APIs. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I7f4d7a99aa42f7f3e4f49d034f8358a41ed42d0f">I7f4d7</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/247708726">b/247708726</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/255352203">b/255352203</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/253043481">b/253043481</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/247716483">b/247716483</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/254529934">b/254529934</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/251840112">b/251840112</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/251859987">b/251859987</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/257141589">b/257141589</a>)</li>
<li>Added in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">IsContainer</code> semantics property on Surfaces. This property will be used in a later change that determines traversal order based on the semantic meaning of elements such as surfaces. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I63379fde102abbee7d5464c50b1c86a59e01e768">I63379</a>)</li>
<li>Added a new accessibility role <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DropdownList</code>. This can be used to replicate <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TalkBack</code>&#39;s behavior when focusing <code translate="no" dir="ltr">android.widget.Spinner</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I177e52da7f2e3c1f9b3d6848bf08a42995b6fb6e">I177e5</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/236159001">b/236159001</a>)</li>
<li>You can now use <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PlatformTextStyle(emojiSupportMatch)</code> to optionally disable emoji support processing for a single Paragraph. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ia710096395ecfe4bbd986326882331e0a7e6a74d">Ia7100</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/139326806">b/139326806</a>)</li>
<li>Android Compose UI tests will now run layout passes for each frame when executing frames to get to idle (e.g. via <code translate="no" dir="ltr">waitForIdle</code>). This may affect tests that assert on individual frames of layout animations. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I8ea08728a395665f9ec7965579797e537b2c35e5">I8ea08</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/222093277">b/222093277</a>)</li>
<li>Added experimental <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TextMotion</code> to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TextStyle</code> to define Text either to be <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Static(default)</code> or Animated. Use <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TextMotion.Animated</code> if Text is going to be scaled, translated, or rotated via animation. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I24dd75e606184220ed3eebc3c80f84d5c977c14c">I24dd7</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.4.0-rc01" data-text="Version 1.4.0-rc01" tabindex="-1">Version 1.4.0-rc01</h3>

<p>March 8, 2023</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.ui:ui-*:1.4.0-rc01</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/87533b4ff06971ed59028936cd9b6da988cd4522..6022301db806601f282c53b8cbb5a981923a1589/compose/ui">Version 1.4.0-rc01 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Added an overload of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">AndroidView</code> composable function, which accepts the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">onReset</code> param. It allows View instances to be reused when their node in the composition is discarded and reused in a compatible way. This is especially useful for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LazyRows</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LazyColumns</code> of Views. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I3f10db5de1b7699964274e0d25f4aad324865dca">I3f10d</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/230099236">b/230099236</a>)</li>
<li>Introduced new low-level <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PlatformTextInputAdapter</code> API for building custom text input implementations that talk directly to platform APIs. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I58df46daa7a88f9761dcd711519c6eddf8524b6d">I58df4</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">BasicTextField</code>&#39;s <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SetText</code> semantics action will now update the text buffer using the same code path as IME updates and the testing functions (e.g. <code translate="no" dir="ltr">performTextReplacement</code>).</li>
<li>Text testing functions <code translate="no" dir="ltr">performTextClearance</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">performTextReplacement</code>, and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">performTextSelection</code> now use <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SemanticsActions</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I0807d73975224ac5bf02fc232c1ab615f76c1c7d">I0807d</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/269633168">b/269633168</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/269624358">b/269624358</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.4.0-beta02" data-text="Version 1.4.0-beta02" tabindex="-1">Version 1.4.0-beta02</h3>

<p>February 22, 2023</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.ui:ui-*:1.4.0-beta02</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/f7337eab774a6ce3b17367d5f31708564b66e677..87533b4ff06971ed59028936cd9b6da988cd4522/compose/ui">Version 1.4.0-beta02 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Removed the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">modifierElementOf()</code> API. Please extend from <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ModifierNodeElement</code> directly instead. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I2256b1776e00cbe0b781dbd7fb483e6740cdb7bc">I2256b</a>)</li>
<li>Added a new <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Modifier.Node.onReset()</code> callback allowing you to reset some local state to properly handle the case when the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Layout</code> will be reused (for example as an item of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LazyColumn</code>). Fixed <code translate="no" dir="ltr">FocusTargetModifierNode</code> to properly reset the focused state. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I65495712cdeafeb3fedc3e4272627c024f952ddb">I65495</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/265201972">b/265201972</a>)</li>
<li>Added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">BlendMode</code> parameter to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DrawScope.drawText</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Paragraph.paint</code>, and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">MultiParagraph.paint</code> methods to support different blending algorithms when drawing text on Canvas. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I57508ab06da481f63b4061ecb8ad72c3a733b0a7">I57508</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Accessibility focus order algorithm improved, for example top/bottom bars are more often read first/last respectively (<a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+/74e9c5f21c148a8c68372c1fae290cd733dd0f46">74e9c5</a>) </li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.4.0-beta01" data-text="Version 1.4.0-beta01" tabindex="-1">Version 1.4.0-beta01</h3>

<li>Added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">waitUntilNodeCount</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">waitUntilAtLeastOneExists</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">waitUntilExactlyOneExists</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">waitUntilDoesNotExist</code> as experimental API to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ComposeTestRule</code>, extending the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">waitUntil</code> API to accept any matcher and any count of nodes. <h3 id="1.4.0-alpha05" data-text="Version 1.4.0-alpha05" tabindex="-1">Version 1.4.0-alpha05</h3>

<h3 id="1.4.0-alpha04" data-text="Version 1.4.0-alpha04" tabindex="-1">Version 1.4.0-alpha04</h3>

<p>January 11, 2023</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.ui:ui-*:1.4.0-alpha04</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/047e199bdcb8a5cd744cc7a2f986631bfb350ec7..adf1c279a86ab3886e1666c08e2c3efba783367b/compose/ui">Version 1.4.0-alpha04 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>New Features</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Added a new <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PinnableContainer</code> API that allows lazy list items to be pinned, so that they are not disposed when they are scrolled out of bounds. For example, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Modifier.focusable()</code> uses this mechanism to pin the currently focused item. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ib8881191a529c9d9dc5e886570650b1987763207">Ib8881</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/259274257">b/259274257</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/195049010">b/195049010</a>)</li>
<li>The focus system is rewritten using the new experimental <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Modifier.Node</code> APIs. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I7f4d7a99aa42f7f3e4f49d034f8358a41ed42d0f">I7f4d7</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/247708726">b/247708726</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/255352203">b/255352203</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/253043481">b/253043481</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/247716483">b/247716483</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/254529934">b/254529934</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/251840112">b/251840112</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/251859987">b/251859987</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/257141589">b/257141589</a>)</li>
<li>Added in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">IsContainer</code> semantics property on Surfaces. This property will be used in a later change that determines traversal order based on the semantic meaning of elements such as surfaces. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I63379fde102abbee7d5464c50b1c86a59e01e768">I63379</a>)</li>
<li>Added new accessibility role <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DropdownList</code>.  This can be used to replicate <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TalkBack&#39;s</code> behavior when focusing <code translate="no" dir="ltr">android.widget.Spinner</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I177e52da7f2e3c1f9b3d6848bf08a42995b6fb6e">I177e5</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/236159001">b/236159001</a>)</li>
<li>You can now use <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PlatformTextStyle(emojiSupportMatch)</code> to optionally disable emoji support processing for a single Paragraph. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ia710096395ecfe4bbd986326882331e0a7e6a74d">Ia7100</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/139326806">b/139326806</a>)</li>
<li>Android Compose UI tests will now run layout passes for each frame when executing frames to get to idle (e.g. via <code translate="no" dir="ltr">waitForIdle</code>). This may affect tests that assert on individual frames of layout animations. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I8ea08728a395665f9ec7965579797e537b2c35e5">I8ea08</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/222093277">b/222093277</a>)</li>
<li>Added experimental <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TextMotion</code> to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TextStyle</code> to define Text either to be <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Static(default)</code> or Animated. Use <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TextMotion.Animated</code> if Text is going to be scaled, translated, or rotated via animation. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I24dd75e606184220ed3eebc3c80f84d5c977c14c">I24dd7</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Replaced <code translate="no" dir="ltr">maxSize: IntSize</code> argument in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">drawText</code> with <code translate="no" dir="ltr">size: Size</code> to be inline with other <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DrawScope</code> functions. <code translate="no" dir="ltr">size</code> is set to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Size.Unspecified</code> by default which should not change the previous default behavior. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Icd27ddc109548e76c7bc4fba08fb9dfc174afa40">Icd27d</a>)</li>
<li>Removed deprecated experimental font constructor. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I8a7245a0eb552b0df8c6bc9344451ccca0d2d2b1">I8a724</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/261435386">b/261435386</a>)</li>
<li>The ui tooling data class <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Group</code> now has a field, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">isInline</code>, that indicates if the group is for a call to an inline composable function. If <code translate="no" dir="ltr">isInline</code> is <code translate="no" dir="ltr">true</code> then the call is to an inline composable function. However, the value might be false for calls to inline composable functions that are from modules that are compiled with a version of the compose compiler plugin that doesn&#39;t generate the inline function information. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Idb84635d4b427de2c4636792307f7e60360a9f0a">Idb846</a>)</li>
<li>Graduated a number of previously experimental APIs to stable</li>
<li>Rotary Scroll Event API is now stable (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I42ad3a466855a165c905dc9e965d140da7269636">I42ad3</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/261561229">b/261561229</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">FontVariation</code> API is now stable (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I8779f6f3097b3e7f6a8596ba65d6f2b4b1d7f2ed">I8779f</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/241016309">b/241016309</a>)</li>
<li>All <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Font()</code> constructors are now stable API (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I5948b7d635d649e93a14e7b4f34ea0a05cd6c3b0">I5948b</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/261435386">b/261435386</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">DeviceFontFamilyName</code> is now stable (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I8b640d1d7880dcd7c581f53ff71baf2af0e80860">I8b640</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/261435386">b/261435386</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">AndroidFont</code> constructor with <code translate="no" dir="ltr">variationSettings</code> is now a stable API, and can be used to create new types of font descriptors. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I5adcc8bd923050d20021d4725fcfe0b36f258ae1">I5adcc</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/261565807">b/261565807</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">createFontFamilyResolver</code> API is now stable. This can be used to catch uncaught exceptions during async font loading. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ibb481cae9c40a1e3ed26e7da911be24fab1788b6">Ibb481</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/261435386">b/261435386</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">Font.loadingStrategy</code> API is now stable. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I5937cfa2e03047eb3affd2c07fb4f75eb35faa97">I5937c</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/261435386">b/261435386</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">GoogleFont</code> API is now stable. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ic90b0bcd8fa3901cc56a9a58979bce25eeded283">Ic90b0</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/261435386">b/261435386</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">TextUnit(float, TextUnitType)</code> is now stable API. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I90c84bd2043c9da0e2fcfa5b4f9fe6ee803d211f">I90c84</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/261561612">b/261561612</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">pluralStringResource</code> is now stable API. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I09849dc71f6203002ad466db12700c2691684e2e">I09849</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/261439703">b/261439703</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.4.0-alpha03" data-text="Version 1.4.0-alpha03" tabindex="-1">Version 1.4.0-alpha03</h3>

<p>December 7, 2022</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.ui:ui-*:1.4.0-alpha03</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/a1e318590b217ecfce1b2de17eed2f18b6a680bb..047e199bdcb8a5cd744cc7a2f986631bfb350ec7/compose/ui">Version 1.4.0-alpha03 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Removing <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ExperimentalComposeUiApi</code> from <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PointerIcon</code> (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I23af8c12762d9baac9864ba93e34d29709027f2a">I23af8</a>)</li>
<li>Introduce Page accessibility actions: <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PageUp</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PageDown</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PageLeft</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PageRight</code>. Note that these are only available from API 29. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ida4ab069a2c7f8d2fc06bf20555c611f4a360728">Ida4ab</a>)</li>
<li>Updated <code translate="no" dir="ltr">rememberNestedScrollConnection</code> parameter view from root view to host view. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ia520073cedb35bffefd54f05bbac186c48521802">Ia5200</a>)</li>
<li>Added an Modifier API to query ancestors scroll info. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I2ba9d6d55f853e5d2775fe9a9f15e7a41d41e359">I2ba9d</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/203141462">b/203141462</a>)</li>
<li>Used in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Clickable</code> to correctly delay press interactions, when gestures could become scroll events.</li>
<li>Fixed <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Clickables</code> not correctly delaying ripples, when used inside an <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Scrollable ViewGroup</code>.</li>
<li>Updated Drawers and Sheets to correctly delay presses in case gestures can become scroll events.</li>
<li>Renamed <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CompositingStrategy.Always</code> to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Offscreen</code> to indicate that the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">graphicsLayer</code> will always be rendered into an intermediate buffer (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I47dc13a167f51d98e9a46ca9bc57209e43a5b18a">I47dc1</a>)</li>
<li>Layout overload with multiple content slots is now stable (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I105661f5ff4127215110cfb53fa437e444088f79">I10566</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/248294649">b/248294649</a>)</li>
<li>Added experimental new APIs <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PerfettoTrace.record {}</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PerfettoTraceRule</code> to capture Perfetto traces (also known as System Traces) as part of a test, to inspect test behavior and performance. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I3ba165beded0d8aabde791e3ac1b786d415404ed">I3ba16</a>)</li>
<li>In UI tests using a Compose rule, continuations resumed during <code translate="no" dir="ltr">withFrameNanos</code> callbacks will not be dispatched until after all frame callbacks have finished running. This matches the behavior of compose when running normally. However, tests that rely on the old behavior may fail. This should only affect code that calls <code translate="no" dir="ltr">withFrameNanos</code> or <code translate="no" dir="ltr">withFrameMillis</code> directly, and has logic outside of callback passed to those functions that may need to be moved inside the callbacks. See the animation test changes in this CL for examples.</li>
<li>Added optional <code translate="no" dir="ltr">onPerformTraversals: (Long) -&gt; Unit</code> parameter to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TestMonotonicFrameClock</code> constructor and factory function to run code after <code translate="no" dir="ltr">withFrameNanos</code> callbacks but before resuming callers&#39; coroutines. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Idb41309445a030c91e8e4ae05daa9642b450505c">Idb413</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/254115946">b/254115946</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/222093277">b/222093277</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/255802670">b/255802670</a>)</li>
<li>Added EmojiCompat to Compose (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ibf6f9f9d37c6280fe1b051269b127f0dfb1d6b6a">Ibf6f9</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/139326806">b/139326806</a>)</li>
<li>Added new wallpaper parameter to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">@Preview</code> for dynamic colour support (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I9f512178c957f6a70f92116ce3dd5394f74131dd">I9f512</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Snapshot apply notifications are now sent after the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Recomposer</code> finishes applying changes. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Iad6c0dcd163a5a8f9c5aec426da3d4f701ca509f">Iad6c0</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/222093277">b/222093277</a>)</li>
<li>Introduced changes in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">captureToImage</code> to allow for capturing multi window screenshots. This is useful for screenshot tests that use compose PopUps. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I169c594f68e20939c98e8ebe0961625140177754">I169c5</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Dependency Updates</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Compose UI and Compose Material now depend on Lifecycle 2.5.1. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I05ab08e48f49eee1a1e573d172ba22efc47640a6">I05ab0</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/258038814">b/258038814</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.4.0-alpha02" data-text="Version 1.4.0-alpha02" tabindex="-1">Version 1.4.0-alpha02</h3>

<p>November 9, 2022</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.ui:ui-*:1.4.0-alpha02</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/548c8ac2570ae6cf15798fea1380491f7d93796b..a1e318590b217ecfce1b2de17eed2f18b6a680bb/compose/ui">Version 1.4.0-alpha02 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Updated <code translate="no" dir="ltr">GraphicsLayerScope</code> to expose the current size of the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">graphicsLayer</code>. This is useful for computing <code translate="no" dir="ltr">graphicsLayer</code> transformations as a function of the Composable size. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/If8c43dad95441ba7cc7ddc845bfa502cce688c7b">If8c43</a>,<a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/181387080">b/181387080</a>)</li>
<li>Introduced <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CompositingStrategy</code> to determine when to leverage an offscreen compositing layer for rendering of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">graphicsLayer</code> content. Auto maintains the default behavior which internally leverages a layer if alpha is applied or a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">RenderEffect/Overscroll</code>. Always will always introduce an offscreen buffer where <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ModulateAlpha</code> will avoid leveraging an offscreen buffer and instead will modulate each of the recorded drawing instructions within the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">graphicsLayer</code>. <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ModulateAlpha</code> usage will still leverage an offscreen buffer for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">RenderEffect/Overscroll</code> usages (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I25e82c7d302e2ffd9353373595a72b8b10627a37">I25e82</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/256382834">b/256382834</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">invalidateSubtree()</code> was added to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Modifier.Node</code> to allow invalidating entire hierarchies for layout and drawing. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I4bd90727827d98f95f4ae4db9032a79dbba2fa33">I4bd90</a>)</li>
<li>Promote <code translate="no" dir="ltr">rememberNestedScrollInteropConnection</code> to stable. Introduced the ability to pass a root view to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">rememberNestedScrollInteropConnection</code>. This can help the custom view better react to scrolling constraints, specially in non-standard views (e.g. <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ModalBottomSheetDialog</code>). (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I9e10769a50354aad1decadaa80152a3814c4480e">I9e107</a>)</li>
<li>Added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ObserverNode</code> interface that can be used by <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Modifier.Node</code> implementations that need to be notified when a value that they had previously read has changed (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I5728be00aad7c3fb9e44240c257f4d45a081da6f">I5728b</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/247716483">b/247716483</a>)</li>
<li>Added a new constructor to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Paint</code> that accepts a native <code translate="no" dir="ltr">android.graphics.Paint</code>. Also added an extension function <code translate="no" dir="ltr">toComposePaint()</code> that converts an existing native Paint object to Compose Paint. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ica91bfd4d1e2215cb0778c173c02f06c3f23fd9d">Ica91b</a>)</li>
<li>Add new <code translate="no" dir="ltr">FontFamily.Resolver.resolveAsTypeface</code> for use on Android. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I8950b91fc2a4edd52c66626c708c413e6d799dfd">I8950b</a>)</li>
<li>Add <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ToolingState</code> to allow tooling to change internal states of Composable (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ie66147788cfde7ede84a94d9591b3a05c51209cb">Ie6614</a>)</li>
<li>Refactor tooling to have better support for new added animations (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I8677b632c114f596a49e2a8d86a16f150feccd6a">I8677b</a>)</li>
<li>Added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">minLines</code> parameter into material and material3 Text, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TextField</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">OutlinedTextField</code> which allows setting the minimum height of the component in terms of number of lines (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I4af1df6521acaa97edbed5048079b5e81b647dd8">I4af1d</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.4.0-alpha01" data-text="Version 1.4.0-alpha01" tabindex="-1">Version 1.4.0-alpha01</h3>

<p>October 24, 2022</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.ui:ui-*:1.4.0-alpha01</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/e6ab75d133443eb5c1d92f910f625741041fc591..548c8ac2570ae6cf15798fea1380491f7d93796b/compose/ui">Version 1.4.0-alpha01 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>A new method, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">awaitEachGesture()</code>, for gesture detectors was added. It operates similar to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">forEachGesture()</code>, but the loop over gestures operates entirely within the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">AwaitPointerEventScope</code> so events can&#39;t be lost between iterations.</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">forEachGesture()</code> has been deprecated in favor of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">awaitEachGesture()</code> because it allows events to be lost between gestures. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Iffc3fb8cf53d0e5eb9b529c023b3e2d29003e86f">Iffc3f</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/251260206">b/251260206</a>)</li>
<li>Deprecating recycling of acccessibility objects in androidx. We&#39;ve found performance changes to be negligible in even the oldest supported versions. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I0a961c85c260b1e8dd97826d0b32c0bdcb51fcfe">I0a961</a>)</li>
<li>Added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DrawStyle</code> as an Experimental attribute to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TextStyle</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SpanStyle</code> to enable drawing outlined text. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/If24b8510daa597283c9f4d39c590747ebd822d69">If24b8</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/155421273">b/155421273</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">AnnotatedString.Builder</code> now implements <code translate="no" dir="ltr">kotlin.text.Appendable</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I1a061f42c46b21f00320b5b31fa717b8d57fd919">I1a061</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/231030444">b/231030444</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">AnnotatedString.Builder</code> now has an <code translate="no" dir="ltr">append(AnnotatedString, start: Int, end: Int)</code> method to append a substring of an <code translate="no" dir="ltr">AnnotatedString</code> and the intersecting styles.</li>
<li>Added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DrawStyle</code> parameter to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Paragraph</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">MultiParagraph</code> paint functions that enables drawing outlined text. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ic8102680bd95cd65f03bac4f3b866e3df637cacf">Ic8102</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/155421273">b/155421273</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>External Contribution</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Thanks for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">vighnesh</code> for adding TV Devices to Previews (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ie15cdcac3aad5c3d191d0ef9a096784549d0460f">Ie15cd</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.3.0" data-text="Version 1.3.0" tabindex="-1">Version 1.3.0</h3>

<p>October 24, 2022</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.ui:ui-*:1.3.0</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/3c2d5397fb8ef697bb04bfc7e98721e2dc0aa255..b5cb4dae1f526ce2408f450b50ade8708684b2be/compose/ui">Version 1.3.0 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>Important changes since 1.2.0</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>New experimental API suite <a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/c/platform/frameworks/support/+/1961800"><code translate="no" dir="ltr">LookaheadLayout</code></a> (enabling previously impossible animation behaviors)</li>
<li>New experimental API suite <a href="/jetpack/androidx/releases/(/jetpack/androidx/releases/compose-ui#1.3.0-beta01)"><code translate="no" dir="ltr">Modifier.Node</code></a> (higher-performance alternative to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Modifier.composed</code>)</li>
<li>Improved window insets support.</li>
<li>Focus support for D-Pads and hardware keyboard in LazyLists.</li>
<li>Maximum supported elevation in dialogs and popups has been reduced to 8dp (behavior breaking change for some customized design systems – <a href="/jetpack/androidx/releases/compose-ui#1.3.0-beta01">rationale in beta01 release notes</a>)</li>
<li>Many <a href="/jetpack/androidx/releases/compose-ui#1.3.0-alpha03">minor, nonbreaking API improvements</a></li>
<li>Many bugfixes and performance improvements</li>
</ul>
