<h3 id="1.1.0-alpha06" data-text="Version 1.1.0-alpha06" tabindex="-1">Version 1.1.0-alpha06</h3>

<p>October 13, 2021</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.ui:ui-*:1.1.0-alpha06</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/da9716386798fc4e39075f54e5bd3317384a63e6..db0888af4fa9a8eaeaf55cc1f120724bc67bdb20/compose/ui">Version 1.1.0-alpha06 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Remove <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ExperimentalComposeUiApi</code> from <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ViewRootForInspector</code>
and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LayoutInfo.ownerViewId</code> (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I5c2e3ad58a1baacb7d329eea216dd56eea548efe">I5c2e3</a>)</li>
<li>A child-less overload for Layout was added, with improved efficiency (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ib0d9a0f11936c0568d20e26a3c6eaa3f938e0ccd">Ib0d9a</a>)</li>
<li>Removed <code translate="no" dir="ltr">InternalCompilerApi</code> from Composer methods that are
required to be called cross-module (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I1aa0b78dbfb808d352e3a46de2388797548d34a9">I1aa0b</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">SemanticsNodeInteraction.performSemanticsAction</code> now returns
the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SemanticsNodeInteraction</code> on which the function was called. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I9e5db630fbc3c254a4cc862c45bae71496e3c99f">I9e5db</a>)</li>
<li>Added LocalInputModeManager CompositionLocal to detect TouchMode/NonTouchMode. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I6a83c0c04f4da63ffdf287051a2277cb337d7104">I6a83c</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/175899786">b/175899786</a>)</li>
<li>Added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">viewConfiguration: ViewConfiguration</code> to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LayoutInfo</code>
to allow consumers get the correct value for things like long press
timeout. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I76ca6fd7a1f9f3161e0ceaee75e4d3431da11251">I76ca6</a>)
<ul>
<li>Added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">viewConfiguration: ViewConfiguration</code> to
<code translate="no" dir="ltr">InjectionScope</code> to allow tests to adjust input injection based on
things like long press timeout or touch slop.</li>
<li>Changed default duration of long press and double tap for both
touch and mouse input to be based on the values in
<code translate="no" dir="ltr">InjectionScope.viewConfiguration</code>.</li>
</ul></li>
<li>Implementation of ExposedDropdownMenu based on ExposedDropdownMenuBox with TextField and DropdownMenu inside (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/If60b2e6c7c139d4d4c134c714e2803f531a6c72a">If60b2</a>)</li>
<li>dismissOnOutsideClick was added to PopupProperties, replacing dismissOnClickOutside which was deprecated. The new property receives the click position and the anchor bounds, providing finer control over whether onDismissRequest should be invoked or not. For example, this can be useful to prevent anchor dismissal for touches on the anchor.
<ul>
<li>updateAndroidWindowManagerFlags was added to PopupProperties, offering low-level control over the flags passed by the popup to the Android WindowManager. The parameter of the lambda will be the flags calculated from the PopupProperties values that result in WindowManager flags: e.g. focusable. The result of the lambda will be the final flags which will be passed to the Android WindowManager. By default, updateAndroidWindowManagerFlags will leave the flags calculated from parameters unchanged. This API should be used with caution, only in cases where the popup has very specific behavior requirements. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I6e9f9d393dc12bd1ea7ae294af1761817f154735">I6e9f9</a>)</li>
</ul></li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">Recomposer.state</code> has been deprecated and replaced by
<code translate="no" dir="ltr">Recomposer.currentState</code> to change its type to a StateFlow (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ic2ab34c19176704fe2f6cd081607dfb92d86ea3c">Ic2ab3</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/197773820">b/197773820</a>)</li>
<li>Added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">flush()</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">dispose()</code> to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">InjectionScope</code>. Use them
when you want to flush all queued up events immediately and when you
want to dispose of the scope, respectively. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ifb73a2812da448c872ab86fc06be4f8c242960b3">Ifb73a</a>)</li>
<li>Added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">performScrollToNode(matcher: SemanticsMatcher)</code> that
scrolls a scrollable container to the content that is matched by the
given matcher. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ic1cb855e351c7bb683962d618d68782628b70f62">Ic1cb8</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">InjectionScope</code> now implements <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Density</code>, allowing you to
easily convert between px and dp in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">performTouchInput</code> and friends. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I8fe1f17d53f8a51f9cb8bcce5b6d40de093da66b">I8fe1f</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>AndroidView now propagates LocalLifecycleOwner and
  LocalSavedStateRegistryOwner to its view via ViewTreeLifecycleOwner
  and ViewTreeSavedStateRegistryOwner. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I38f966576085db66e35b0106f49275ef5bb31adc">I38f96</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/179708470">b/179708470</a>)</li>
<li>Fix WearOS SwipeToDismissBox sometimes not handling swipes. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I9387e6584e9d04d7ffda3a4319e3da2da13788b5">I9387e</a>)</li>
<li>The default time between injected input events has been
changed from 10ms to 16ms. This potentially changes the outcome of tests
that perform input gestures, like a specific swipe. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I829fd33dd4ba14313ac73daf7c2e770955c90df6">I829fd</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.1.0-alpha05" data-text="Version 1.1.0-alpha05" tabindex="-1">Version 1.1.0-alpha05</h3>

<p>September 29, 2021</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.ui:ui-*:1.1.0-alpha05</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/1a3dcfb231517d6104969f17063fcc6c97ba6eeb..da9716386798fc4e39075f54e5bd3317384a63e6/compose/ui">Version 1.1.0-alpha05 contains these commits.</a></p>

<li>Added experimental historical pointers to PointerEventChange. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ic1fd82fd3f2335a9289cc1fc96c35e89ec9b90ee">Ic1fd8</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/197553056">b/197553056</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/199921305">b/199921305</a>)</li>

LayoutDirection</code> to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LayoutInfo</code>. This allows consumers of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LayoutInfo</code>
to interpret the dimensions and position exposed in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LayoutInfo</code>
properly. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I002f191f17be7fa867cecf9c974edfb694523786">I002f1</a>)</li>

through the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Mouse</code> property of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">MultiModalInjectionScope</code> during a
multi modal input gesture with <code translate="no" dir="ltr">performMultiModalInput</code>. See
<code translate="no" dir="ltr">MouseInjectionScope</code> for documentation of the available API. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Iaa4a82131f35d2d6376d8edaa1fac4807b27045d">Iaa4a8</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/190493367">b/190493367</a>)</li>

<li>Improved <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TouchInjectionScope.swipeWithVelocity</code>. It now
accepts a wider range of input variables and will suggest changes to the

<h3 id="1.1.0-alpha04" data-text="Version 1.1.0-alpha04" tabindex="-1">Version 1.1.0-alpha04</h3>

<p>September 15, 2021</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.ui:ui-*:1.1.0-alpha04</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/bf63d633b292368932b7ea1994e4116f95a94b5c..1a3dcfb231517d6104969f17063fcc6c97ba6eeb/compose/ui">Version 1.1.0-alpha04 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">PointerEvent</code> now has a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PointerEventType</code>
to support hover events. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I091fa991d1680d69a2532e73a894913c2865663d">I091fa</a>)</li>
<li>Allow children to accept pointer input outside of
parent&#39;s pointer input bounds. Parents may intercept those
calls with a property PointerInputScope.alwaysInterceptChildEvents (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I9eae3ce577012e26c3532266ac63db8e84ce5c7f">I9eae3</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/192479655">b/192479655</a>)</li>
<li>Deprecated <code translate="no" dir="ltr">performGesture</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">GestureScope</code>, which have
been replaced by <code translate="no" dir="ltr">performTouchInput</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TouchInjectionScope</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ia5f3f740c51a1add60fa82189d583d8a5192dd31">Ia5f3f</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/190493367">b/190493367</a>)</li>
<li>Added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">touchBoundsInRoot</code> to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SemanticsNode</code> that
includes the minimum touch target size so that developers
can ensure that touch targets meet accessibility minimums. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I2e14bf1bab7a745aa2421353f44c734540d2489c">I2e14b</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/197751214">b/197751214</a>)</li>
<li>Redo implementation of inspectable (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I927bc731712d81f47aefdf946f778047c7645b26">I927bc</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/191017532">b/191017532</a>)</li>
<li>Changed parameter name of inspectable to match composed (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I3a482c9f64ef0f7cc5a5a59cecaec010ca001e3f">I3a482</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/191017532">b/191017532</a>)</li>
<li><p>Introduced <code translate="no" dir="ltr">performTouchInput</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TouchInjectionScope</code> as a
replacement for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">performTouchInput</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TouchInjectionScope</code>, paving
the way for other modalities (like mouse).</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">TouchInjectionScope</code> has the same methods as <code translate="no" dir="ltr">GestureScope</code>, with the
exception of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">movePointerTo</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">movePointerBy</code>, which have been
renamed to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">updatePointerTo</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">updatePointerBy</code>. All other methods
are the same.</p>

<p>The behavior of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TouchInjectionScope</code> is almost identical to
<code translate="no" dir="ltr">GestureScope</code>, with two small details:</p>

<ol>
<li>When sending a down event while pointers had been moved without
sending a move event (in other words, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">updatePointerTo()</code> has been
used, but not <code translate="no" dir="ltr">move()</code>, and then <code translate="no" dir="ltr">down()</code> is called), the previous
implementation would advance the event time and send a move event
before sending the down event. The new implementation still sends the
move event, but doesn&#39;t advance the event time in this specific
scenario.</li>
<li>When sending an up event while pointers had been moved without
sending a move event (similar as above), the previous implementation
would advance the event time and send a move event before sending the
up event. The new implementation does neither: the new positions of
the pointers will only be reflected through the up event.</li>
</ol>

<p>Finally, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TouchInjectionScope</code> introduces a new method
<code translate="no" dir="ltr">currentPosition(pointerId: Int)</code> to get the current position of the
given pointer. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/If11912d1d85da53b0f675f874be29ecde1b8c7cd">If1191</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/190493367">b/190493367</a>)</p></li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Allow clip to extend touch target bounds beyond
the clip region for minimum touch target purposes. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I43e10218f7a20b5a8190ea838cef8eb8440928d1">I43e10</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/171509422">b/171509422</a>)</li>
<li>Support for stretch overscroll has been added on Android 12 devices. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Iccf3c3830a01469940828e21bc32b569951c187e">Iccf3c</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/171682480">b/171682480</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.1.0-alpha03" data-text="Version 1.1.0-alpha03" tabindex="-1">Version 1.1.0-alpha03</h3>

<p>September 1, 2021</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.ui:ui-*:1.1.0-alpha03</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/1e0ab9e58c3c2ebe8152b7507938aef7e9c1acdc..bf63d633b292368932b7ea1994e4116f95a94b5c/compose/ui">Version 1.1.0-alpha03 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>New Features</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Updated Compose <code translate="no" dir="ltr">1.1.0-alpha03</code> to depend on Kotlin <code translate="no" dir="ltr">1.5.30</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I74545c317093029a2a46707b9024ad3385854ecb">I74545</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Modifier.inspectable</code> for wrapping other modifiers. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I1909b068b72041b8363c04c7ec619fcf26702da4">I1909b</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/191017532">b/191017532</a>)</li>
<li>Added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">BlurredEdgeTreatment</code> API
to simplify blur use cases into more
commonly used combinations of clip flags
and TileModes. Most use cases involve
either letting blurred content render
outside the original content bounds
and blurring regions outside these bounds
with transparent black, or clipping content
to content bounds sampling the closest edge
for blur kernels that extend beyond content
bounds. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I6b4b7966920855374275ae7ea950b310fa28efd0">I6b4b7</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/166927547">b/166927547</a>)</li>
<li>Added support for RenderEffect
in compose desktop.
Introduced OffsetEffect as well as
the blur modifier as a simple way to
introduce blur visual effects to a portion
of the composition hierarchy. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I0f6aa293db2bf34f5ed2aa7499a97332dacf73fc">I0f6aa</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/166927547">b/166927547</a>)</li>
<li>Introduced RenderEffect API
that can be optionally configured on
a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Modifier.graphicsLayer</code> to alter
the contents of the layer itself. This
can be used to blur contents of a composable
and child composables within a composition
hierarchy. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I47c4d5ecc801f35e632d2062e03c756f564a2db5">I47c4d</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/166927547">b/166927547</a>)</li>
<li>AwaitPointerEventScope now has withTimeout()
and withTimeoutOrNull() (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I507f0e696311ac0504126681c376f73beaa021fb">I507f0</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/179239764">b/179239764</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/182397793">b/182397793</a>)</li>
<li>Added minimum touch target size to ViewConfiguration
for use in semantics and pointer input to ensure accessibility. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ie861ca1fcdbfcc9455352fc3a459d5734d5d57cc">Ie861c</a>)</li>
<li>Add TileMode.Decal support
which is useful in defining edge
behavior for blur based RenderEffects. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I7e8ed0c4eb2490ef3cd0032b5952d0962f489354">I7e8ed</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/166927547">b/166927547</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">performScrollToIndex</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">performScrollToKey</code>,
<code translate="no" dir="ltr">hasScrollToIndexAction</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">hasScrollToKeyAction</code> are now stable API (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I142aefdd8455195d30a6b029b76255f1f737939f">I142ae</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/178483889">b/178483889</a>)</li>
<li>Added test method to get the clipped bounds. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I6b28e437d6893a63be65c8a451a84bcb21bce906">I6b28e</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Removed isBounded method
from BlurredEdgeTreatment in favor
of explicitly checking if the shape
parameter is null. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I85d687c2591770875dbfcc0fb893a8a377efefc4">I85d68</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.1.0-alpha02" data-text="Version 1.1.0-alpha02" tabindex="-1">Version 1.1.0-alpha02</h3>

<p>August 18, 2021</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.ui:ui-*:1.1.0-alpha02</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/d725303accfa9be6d5c3d61c7603ed1b9a780cbd..1e0ab9e58c3c2ebe8152b7507938aef7e9c1acdc/compose/ui">Version 1.1.0-alpha02 contains these commits.</a></p>

<ul>
<li>PointerEvent now has support for reading
mouse button state and keyboard modifier state. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I6310c8e6bd4d2e383389db7d4a33299aa1c52cd3">I6310c</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/180075467">b/180075467</a>)</li>
<li>Injected gestures now use the MainTestClock&#39;s time as the
source of truth for time. The current time for injected events in
<code translate="no" dir="ltr">performGesture</code> will be initialized to the current time of the
MainTestClock. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ifb364da90fcbecacfcf7614168969655777905cd">Ifb364</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/192064452">b/192064452</a>)</li>
<li>Added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DpRect(DpOffset, DpSize)</code> constructor (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I2cf1636d05302a444587d6a6c43bd2e52c0a903f">I2cf16</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/194219828">b/194219828</a>)</li>
<li>Added DpSize class (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I7abb129c8c18a3f77b68aec5c2060d2aad11a693">I7abb1</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/194219828">b/194219828</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Updated Vector graphics xml
parsing to support ColorStateLists as
root color tint properties on VectorDrawables. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I86915d08bdf50f729e91ec85c9f8595ad16f9562">I86915</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/195668138">b/195668138</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.1.0-alpha01" data-text="Version 1.1.0-alpha01" tabindex="-1">Version 1.1.0-alpha01</h3>

<p>August 4, 2021</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.ui:ui-*:1.1.0-alpha01</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/1a3ba62b97c98d85f6c0ac2fb6483fc9ac60872e..d725303accfa9be6d5c3d61c7603ed1b9a780cbd/compose/ui">Version 1.1.0-alpha01 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">RelocationRequester.bringIntoView</code> now accepts a rectangle as a parameter which enables us to bring a part of a composable into view (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ice2c55d582bbeb80757cf30e2334bb970a31f438">Ice2c5</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/194330245">b/194330245</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">AnimatedImageVector</code> and the related APIs are now in the new
<code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.animation:animation-graphics</code> module. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I6087391a9869d2315a71422f24175f42ec085681">I60873</a>)</li>
<li>Added experimental modifier to handle relocation requests. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I65a97bd7fca7271781efe31fcc9cb387e9857b51">I65a97</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/178211874">b/178211874</a>)</li>
<li><p>Introduced BrushPainter API
to support drawing of an arbitrary Brush
within a Painter, similar to ColorPainter</p>

<p>Updated Brush API to have an intrinsic size
parameter that is queried within BrushPainter (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ia27529070e6f2acdac9d2c73f41e886b36452f34">Ia2752</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/189466433">b/189466433</a>)</p></li>
<li><p>Updated DrawScope#drawImage method that
consumes source and destination rects
to consume an optional FilterQuality
parameter. This is useful for pixel
art that is intended to be pixelated
when scaled up for pixel based art.
Updated BitmapPainter + Image composable
to also consume an optional FilterQuality
parameter (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ie4fb04013701add0fba1c5c6bb9da2812d6436e7">Ie4fb0</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/180311607">b/180311607</a>)</p></li>
<li><p>Added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">GestureScope.advanceEventTime</code> method to give more
control over the timing of events in a gesture (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ibf3e2d35b4462863aa0de010cb2d0fe0d10cd3d1">Ibf3e2</a>)</p></li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>In order to better support chaining of
draw modifiers, make sure the Modifier.paint implementation
calls drawsContent.
Previously Modifier.paint was expected to a leaf node in
the chain of Modifiers, however, by doing so it prevents
it from being configured on a composable container (ex. box)
or adding additional decorations on top such as
<code translate="no" dir="ltr">Modifier.paint().border()</code>. By having Modifier.paint
call drawContent after drawing the contents of the given
painter, we have better behavior consistency in behavior
with the modifier pattern. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ibb2a7ae54a86643ba4fc1604ce39df7477ab66f0">Ibb2a7</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/178201337">b/178201337</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/186213275">b/186213275</a>)</li>
<li>Dialogs now follow the platform sizing behaviour. Set <code translate="no" dir="ltr">usePlatformDefaultWidth</code> to false to override this behaviour. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Iffaedb8890f59627a58fb4f33d06044ac120fd7d">Iffaed</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/192682388">b/192682388</a>)</li>
<li>Moved <code translate="no" dir="ltr">InfiniteAnimationPolicy</code> to :compose:ui (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I5eb09c7aa24a85fd2e66cc9b84ea6c906dc5210a">I5eb09</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/160602714">b/160602714</a>)</li>
<li>Scrolling via semantics actions for lazy lists and regular scrolling components is now animated (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Id9066420fd80bbea3c0463813be0338fff017514">Id9066</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/190742024">b/190742024</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p>This is the first stable release of Compose.  Please see the official <a href="https://android-developers.googleblog.com/2021/07/jetpack-compose-announcement.html">Compose Release blog</a> for more details!</p>

<p><strong>Known Issues</strong></p>

<ul>
<li><p>If you are using Android Studio Bumblebee Canary 4 or AGP <code translate="no" dir="ltr">7.1.0-alpha04</code>/<code translate="no" dir="ltr">7.1.0-alpha05</code>, you may hit the following crash:</p>
<div></div><devsite-code><pre class="devsite-click-to-copy" translate="no" dir="ltr" is-upgraded syntax="Text only"><code translate="no" dir="ltr">  java.lang.AbstractMethodError: abstract method "void androidx.lifecycle.DefaultLifecycleObserver.onCreate(androidx.lifecycle.LifecycleOwner)"
</code></pre></devsite-code>
<p>To fix, temporarily increase your minSdkVersion to 24+ in your <code translate="no" dir="ltr">build.gradle</code> file.  This issue will be fixed in the next version of Android Studio Bumblebee and AGP <code translate="no" dir="ltr">7.1</code>.  (<a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/194289155">b/194289155</a>)</p></li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.0.0-rc01" data-text="Version 1.0.0-rc01" tabindex="-1">Version 1.0.0-rc01</h3>

<p>July 1, 2021</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.ui:ui-*:1.0.0-rc01</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/f434dccf3dc4d4e82d8d965da3746615870537b4..1a3ba62b97c98d85f6c0ac2fb6483fc9ac60872e/compose/ui">Version 1.0.0-rc01 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>New Features</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Split ui-tooling module into <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ui-tooling</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ui-tooling-preview</code> (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Iefa283aba6e2b41459ea17b0c35a4d6fc7fb4c3f">Iefa28</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/190649014">b/190649014</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Removed deprecated experimental <code translate="no" dir="ltr">FocusManager#moveFocusIn</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">FocusManager#moveFocusOut</code> (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I227d79e985d993d52d383d22439abaecbce9f593">I227d7</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/170154986">b/170154986</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/186567354">b/186567354</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/168510304">b/168510304</a>)</li>
<li>Canvas now supports a contentDescription parameter for
accessibility. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ib547c8fdb4c76a64f5ddcfe8ef3d46a0792f40bc">Ib547c</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">useDefaultMaxWidth</code> in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PopupProperties</code> was renamed to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">usePlatformDefaultWidth</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I0571008fba7541d07511b95f31e1854849f36124">I05710</a>)</li>
<li>Dialogs are now able to use the entire screen width. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I83929941b29e5afe443b7472ff36e46b1ccc8108">I83929</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/190810877">b/190810877</a>)</li>
<li>Added experimental support for HSV and HSL color
representations. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Id7cf8ae76f6fbeaebabcd5551d71964f50499b4a">Id7cf8</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/180731008">b/180731008</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Behavior Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Compose <code translate="no" dir="ltr">@Preview</code> now provides a
<code translate="no" dir="ltr">LocalActivityResultRegistryOwner</code> that allows you
to preview Composables that use APIs like
<code translate="no" dir="ltr">rememberLauncherForActivityResult()</code> that depend
on that owner existing. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ib13d12f085065adb89cfb731179b9295029e06e9">Ib13d1</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/185693006">b/185693006</a>)</li>
<li>Compose <code translate="no" dir="ltr">@Preview</code> now provides a
<code translate="no" dir="ltr">LocalOnBackPressedDispatcherOwner</code> that allows you
to preview Composables that use APIs like <code translate="no" dir="ltr">BackHandler</code>
that depend on that owner existing. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ia1c05ea3cadf2fb55cef9c4b8bae0898cfb35ba9">Ia1c05</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/185693006">b/185693006</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Moved <code translate="no" dir="ltr">InfiniteAnimationPolicy</code> to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.ui:ui</code> (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I5eb09c7aa24a85fd2e66cc9b84ea6c906dc5210a">I5eb09</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/160602714">b/160602714</a>)</li>
<li>AnimatedImageVector was temporarily removed in order to change the module structure. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I419062b1b225003ee594f4d8522b11bb024144d6">I41906</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/160602714">b/160602714</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.0.0-beta09" data-text="Version 1.0.0-beta09" tabindex="-1">Version 1.0.0-beta09</h3>

<p>June 16, 2021</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.ui:ui-*:1.0.0-beta09</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/836237c11d7a415f28bb71acab597579be1d5227..f434dccf3dc4d4e82d8d965da3746615870537b4/compose/ui">Version 1.0.0-beta09 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Change enum Role and LiveRegionMode into inline classes
with private constructor (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Id189080b0537dde66639fc87f08ec5f46a449a97">Id1890</a>)</li>
<li>KeyboardCapitalization is converted into an inline class. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Id5a1c8b2c89a65eb41aa44675b960a3bb0dc1020">Id5a1c</a>)</li>
<li>Change HapticFeedbackType to inline class. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I255ec46ff76414180599fc5328a5b6b57a6f0915">I255ec</a>)</li>
<li>Modifier.pointerInteropFilter is @ExperimentalComposeUiApi. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Iede6c29413d359091df79d8178684c857305db75">Iede6c</a>)</li>
<li>TextAlign, FontSynthesis and TextDirection are now inline
classes. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I212fee8bac36263fb0eda9c3362015c860168a73">I212fe</a>)</li>
<li>TextOverflow is changed to an inline class. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I433af65606ae4e79ea0cb281be7049c73b12fcf0">I433af</a>)</li>
<li>FontStyle is now an inline class. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I9e48bba8f3c4e4cc45468b86d7145b18389be21c">I9e48b</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Key constants are @ExperimentalComposeUiApi for now. Consuming
code can declare private constants prior to stabilization. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ia5d48d518c6e73f5e3458260203dc237bef5464d">Ia5d48</a>)</li>
<li>Compose tests can now be run on Robolectric. The following
limitations have so far been identified:
<ul>
<li>There is no native bitmap, so <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ImageBitmap()</code> leads to a
NullPointerException.</li>
<li>There is no drawing, so <code translate="no" dir="ltr">captureToImage()</code> will indefinitely await the
next draw pass (i.e. it deadlocks).</li>
<li>There is no font loaded, so any text will be measured incorrectly. All
characters have a fixed height of around 20px and width of 1px.</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">ComposeTestRule.waitUntil {}</code> does not run the main thread while it’s waiting, making it effectively the same as <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ComposeTestRule.mainClock.advanceTimeUntil {}</code>
More limitations are expected to be identified in the future. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I284face60a4e5f6942b3d92cac7d47056d8174f3">I284fa</a>)</li>
</ul></li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Added Profile Rules</strong></p>

<p>This release adds profile rules to the following compose modules (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I14ed64578d535320a40ed8d486f75715641b2762">I14ed6</a>):</p>

<ul>
<li>androidx.compose.animation</li>
<li>androidx.compose.animation-core</li>
<li>androidx.compose.foundation</li>
<li>androidx.compose.foundation-layout</li>
<li>androidx.compose.material</li>
<li>androidx.compose.material-ripple</li>
<li>androidx.compose.runtime</li>
<li>androidx.compose.ui</li>
<li>androidx.compose.ui.geometry</li>
<li>androidx.compose.ui.graphics</li>
<li>androidx.compose.ui.text</li>
<li>androidx.compose.ui.text</li>
<li>androidx.compose.ui.unit</li>
<li>androidx.compose.ui.util</li>
</ul>

<h4 id="what_are_profile_rules_2" data-text="What are profile rules?" tabindex="-1">What are profile rules?</h4>

<ul>
<li><p>Profile rules for a library are specified in a text file <code translate="no" dir="ltr">baseline-prof.txt</code> located in the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">src/main</code> or equivalent directory. The file specifies a rule per line, where a rule in this case is a pattern for matching to methods or classes in the library. The syntax for these rules is a superset of the human-readable ART profile format that is used when using <code translate="no" dir="ltr">adb shell profman --dump-classes-and-methods ...</code>. These rules take one of two forms to target either methods or classes.</p></li>
<li><p>A method rule will have the following pattern:</p>
<div></div><devsite-code><pre class="devsite-click-to-copy" translate="no" dir="ltr" is-upgraded syntax="Kotlin"><code translate="no" dir="ltr">&lt;<span class="devsite-syntax-n">FLAGS&gt;&lt;CLASS_DESCRIPTOR&gt;</span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">-</span>&gt;&lt;<span class="devsite-syntax-n">METHOD_SIGNATURE</span>&gt;
</code></pre></devsite-code></li>
<li><p>And a class rule will have the following pattern:</p>
<div></div><devsite-code><pre class="devsite-click-to-copy" translate="no" dir="ltr" is-upgraded syntax="Kotlin"><code translate="no" dir="ltr">&lt;<span class="devsite-syntax-n">CLASS_DESCRIPTOR</span>&gt;
</code></pre></devsite-code></li>
<li><p>Here <code translate="no" dir="ltr">&lt;FLAGS&gt;</code> is one or more of the characters <code translate="no" dir="ltr">H</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">S</code>, and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">P</code> to indicate whether or not this method should be flagged as &quot;Hot&quot;, &quot;Startup&quot;, or &quot;Post Startup&quot;.</p></li>
<li><p>The <code translate="no" dir="ltr">&lt;CLASS_DESCRIPTOR&gt;</code> is the descriptor for the class that the targeted method belongs to. For example, the class <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.runtime.SlotTable</code> would have a descriptor of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Landroidx/compose/runtime/SlotTable;</code>.</p></li>
<li><p>The <code translate="no" dir="ltr">&lt;METHOD_SIGNATURE&gt;</code> is the signature of the method, and includes the name, parameter types, and return types of the method. For example, the method <code translate="no" dir="ltr">fun isPlaced(): Boolean</code> on <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LayoutNode</code> has the signature <code translate="no" dir="ltr">isPlaced()Z</code>.</p></li>
<li><p>These patterns can have wildcards (<code translate="no" dir="ltr">**</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">*</code>, and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">?</code>) in order to have a single rule encompass multiple methods or classes.</p></li>
</ul>

<h4 id="what_do_the_rules_do_2" data-text="What do the rules do?" tabindex="-1">What do the rules do?</h4>

<ul>
<li><p>A method that has the flag <code translate="no" dir="ltr">H</code> indicates that this method is a &quot;hot&quot; method, and should be compiled ahead of time.</p></li>
<li><p>A method that has the flag <code translate="no" dir="ltr">S</code> indicates that it is a method which is called at startup, and should be compiled ahead of time to avoid the cost of compilation and interpreting the method at startup time.</p></li>
<li><p>A method that has the flag <code translate="no" dir="ltr">P</code> indicates that it is a method which is called after startup.</p></li>
<li><p>A class that is present in this file indicates that it is used during startup and should be pre-allocated in the heap to avoid the cost of class loading.</p></li>
</ul>

<h4 id="how_does_this_work_2" data-text="How does this work?" tabindex="-1">How does this work?</h4>

<ul>
<li>Libraries can define these rules which will be packaged in AAR artifacts. When an app is then built which includes these artifacts, these rules are merged together and the merged rules are used to build a compact binary ART profile that is specific to the app. ART can then leverage this profile when the app is installed on devices in order to ahead-of-time compile a specific subset of the application to improve the performance of the application, especially the first run. Note that this will have no effect on debuggable applications.</li>
</ul>

<aside class="note"><strong>Note:</strong><span> Libraries dependent on Compose will need to recompile with version <code translate="no" dir="ltr">1.0.0</code>&#8209;<code translate="no" dir="ltr">beta07</code>. <code translate="no" dir="ltr">java.lang.NoSuchMethodError: No interface method startReplaceableGroup(ILjava/lang/String;)V in class Landroidx/compose/runtime/Composer; or its super classes</code>. <ul>

<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">SubcomposeLayoutState</code> now supports setting count of reusable slots. The layout will keep up to this count slots active instead of disposing them in order to reuse the slot next time we need a new one (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ieb9817249f5fa77ca12d32fcec2747e79c12565e">Ieb981</a>)</li>

(<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ib6d03c672268e89eb67b5f3de7c29763872f5686">Ib6d03</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/187055290">b/187055290</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/184086802">b/184086802</a>)</li>
<li>Introduces ability to hoist the SubcomposeLayout state which allows you to precompose the content into a requires slotId which would make the next measure pass faster as once we try to subcompose with the given slotId next time there will be no composition needed. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I425806be5ec3e36337e04558e6621fbe515b7cd8">I42580</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/184940225">b/184940225</a>)</li>

</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>LazyColumn/Row will now keep up to 2 previously visible items active (not disposed) even when they are scrolled out already. This allows the component to reuse the active subcompositions when we will need to compose a new item which improves the scrolling performance. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ie5555c9a7031dc9bd31f452a0ed9b28d8a337f5f">Ie5555</a>)</li>

scrollable, it will now scroll by one screen in the given direction. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ieccb0a794d61dc5fe28a236b379755d776c023dc">Ieccb0</a>)</li>
<li>The AndroidManifest files from ui-test-manifest and
ui-tooling-data are now compatible with Android 12 (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I6f9dec0515ad6eb7fd232eeb124ee0164f4e90cb">I6f9de</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/184718994">b/184718994</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.0.0-beta04" data-text="Version 1.0.0-beta04" tabindex="-1">Version 1.0.0-beta04</h3>

<p>April 7, 2021</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.ui:ui-*:1.0.0-beta04</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/5c42896eb6591b09e3952030fb7ea8d9b8c42713..0e6e72e136ada934db74265667417524ba0ba04f/compose/ui">Version 1.0.0-beta04 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Rename <code translate="no" dir="ltr">hideSoftwareKeyboard</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">showSoftwareKeyboard</code> on
<code translate="no" dir="ltr">SoftwareKeyboardController</code> to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">hide()</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">show()</code> respectively.
<ul>
<li>Provide the full CompositionLocal interface for
LocalSoftwareKeyboardController, allowing it to be set (especially
useful in tests) (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I579a6e311d1cc96e4ea398465cad3a402a633b8d">I579a6</a>)</li>
</ul></li>
<li>LiveRegion accessibility API is added.
If node is marked as a live region, the accessibility services
will automatically notify the user about its changes (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Idcf6f425b12b005e59ad77fe7430e466132ea87c">Idcf6f</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/172590946">b/172590946</a>)</li>
<li>TextOverflow.Visible is introduced. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ic8f898df15fa7cfa3fadf5a47d5b0e34a68f52f6">Ic8f89</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Fixed the issue when items of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LazyColumn</code>/<code translate="no" dir="ltr">LazyRow</code> located on the edges were incorrectly positioned after fast fling (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ie4d13def7dc4b12d4f52b4c5edbb0abb5150f698">Ie4d13</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/183877420">b/183877420</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">AndroidViewBinding</code> now properly removes
fragments inflated via <code translate="no" dir="ltr">FragmentContainerView</code> when
the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">AndroidViewBinding</code> is removed from the compose
hierarchy. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ib02480f78570972b3190ebd45ab12f4d7291fa23">Ib0248</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/179915946">b/179915946</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">AndroidViewBinding</code> now correctly nests
fragments inflated via <code translate="no" dir="ltr">FragmentContainerView</code> when
your <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ComposeView</code> is within a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Fragment</code>, fixing
issues with saving and restoring the state of those
fragments. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I70eb0831fb6b756e2968e713e181193969d49b9a">I70eb0</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/179915946">b/179915946</a>)</li>
<li>Compose ViewBinding now depends on
<a href="/jetpack/androidx/releases/fragment#1.3.2">Fragment <code translate="no" dir="ltr">1.3.2</code></a>
and now consistently shows fragments inflated via
<code translate="no" dir="ltr">FragmentContainerView</code> after configuration changes. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I0743d383564ee28429ad0074f58de79c0e98ada0">I0743d</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/179915946">b/179915946</a>)</li>
</ul>
